<response>None< /response>< Review>
Best park in San Francisco with a view. Not a lot of people usually. Great place to walk the dog or smooch with your lover. You can take a bus that will get ya close or if in shape truck up the hill it's about a mile from Castro which is a great place for a pick me up or food on your way home  I give this a five star review mainly for the view.<//Review>

<Rate>4</Rate>< Review>
I take my dog here almost every morning. The regular owners are very nice and the dogs are well behaved. There have been a few accidents with aggressive or possessive dogs. Being mindful and knowledgeable of your dog to avoid issues or to separate/leave for the day Is the best choice of action.

Not the best place for small children as some dogs dont like kids or are afraid of them. Keep your child close to you and please ask permission if our larger dogs are okay with being pet.< /Review>

<name>Cam<//name><Time>1559668219680< /Time><gmapID>0x808f7e020f206785:0xa8ba1cd74c4aefb2<//gmapID>< response>
None</response>
<Rate>4<//Rate>< review>
Great place for my group walks, there are hiding places under the vine brush some of my puppies like to play under. It's mostly other walkers there which is nice because my dogs have a whole other group to play with. There's a dog and human fountain outside the enclosed area. And a bucket and hose for the dogs within the enclosed area. The whole area is covered in bark, but when it rains, sometimes the sand and mud can come through. The only think I'd say is a downside to this park is that it seems to attract argument-prone people. Not with me, but I tend to witness it. Besides that, I highly recommend it!<//review>

<rating>5< /rating>< Review>
I had to get my nails done prior to my wedding.  I had literally chewed my nails off due to stress and anxiety and decided to get acrylic nails for the first time.   After asking around, I booked an appointment at this salon.
When I went in for my appointment with Amanda, she was super chill and made helpful suggestions on getting my nails done.  She took her time doing my nails and they came out beautifully.  I was surprised at how well they held up due to I am pretty hard on my nails.  They held up for weeks until I was able to go in for my next appointment to get my first set of fills
This salon is friendly, professional, and clean.  The fact that you have to book an appointment means you have to book your appointment a couple of weeks in advance, but it also means that you are not sitting there waiting for half an hour which has been my experience when getting mani/pedis at salons that take walk ins.</Review>

<Resp>None</Resp><Review>In A Nutshell:

-If you can find parking in the small parking lot, then Com Tam Thien Huong is worth it.
-The interior design is nice, feels upscale.
-They serve other dishes like pho, hu tieu & bun, but they are well-known for their com tam.
-Com tam is "broken rice", which is supposed to be the broken pieces of rice at the bottom of the rice bag that the poor people would end up eating.
-Thankfully, Vietnamese are some of the most clever & best cooks in the world so they definitely make due w/ any ingredient they have at their disposal.
-The com tam served here is very good, nice presentation w/ thinly sliced bbq pork chops.

Overall, if you can find parking then this is a great place to grab some com tam in Little Saigon - San Jose.< /Review><date>1508771622115</date><Rating>4</Rating><pictures>None< /pictures></record></dataset><record>

<rating>4<//rating>< Review>
Awesome place for a walk, bike, or horse ride. You can take a short one mile walk around the lake area or it connects with the entire Rohr Park area. The trails are wide with plenty of space. Reviews are very nice especially right now with all the flowers blooming. Easy to get to and plenty of parking. There are even picnic spots available and benches to sit and look at the lake.</Review>

<Review>Coming into therapy is always a treat. I don't write a ton of reviews - just recently started trying to boost a few of my favorite places over the last few months, and therapy definitely deserves one. Pre-covid, whenever I had happy hours or dinners on Castro, I'd wander into therapy before or after, just to see what goodies they might have. I'd always be amused looking at everything they had.

They have soooo many cute, trendy gifts! You can find things for babies or for the home, books for travel, cooking, or satirical humor, apparel and accessories for women and men, and the softest cutest stuffed animals... just to name a few.. They always change their selection, so you'll always find something new.

To top it off, their staff is ALWAYS so friendly and personable. Just last week, i went to Castro again and was excited to see therapy re-opened. I strolled in and was greeted by the manager on that day- Savannah. She was just full of positive vibes, and it was such a joy to have a conversation with her in the middle of shelter in place. It made me reflect that anytime I bought something from therapy, I always had a genuinely pleasant conversation with each of the staff that rang me up in the past. Needless to say, I always walk out of the store feeling a bit happier.

Therapy- such a suiting name for a store where I find so much therapy :) not just retail therapy, but even positive human-to-human interaction therapy.< /Review>< Rating>

<rate>5<//rate>< Review>
Antime you get involve in a major project, you just never really know who to call. My HVAC system' which was installed in 2002' failed. It was over 103 degrees that day and would be that hot for next few days. I called the original installer of my system. They were quite capable and when this company checked the system, it was time for a new one. Elite got out the house the next day and came to same conclusion.

I called the original installer and they said they would send a rep to go over the cost and set up a time to install. Then the phone rep said that a install couldn't happen for a month. I told them that would not work and thanked them for their time. Enter Elite.

Chianti came to the house and was very low keyed. No pressure, just wanted to show what was needed. I felt comfortable but I had to ask. When can you install? Chianti call Victor, the owner. Victor said that they could install by the end of the week. I told Chianti that I had called another company to look the system over and to quote me a price. In fact, they showed up as Chianti was leaving.

I waited until the next day to compare prices. The second company was more expensive but pushed financing (which I did not need) and the ability to match prices. I thanked them for their time, call Chianti and signed the contract to have Elite install. Great decision on my part.

Three days later at 8:30 am, Logan and Ozzie were at the front door. Showed them to the system and they went to work. They even had a moment or two to play fetch with my dogs! First day, the entire system was removed. Second day, back at 8:30 for the install. That afternoon we had one outstanding HVAC system blowing cold air.

There two guys were great. I asked questions (I work from home), they answered them. They were always in good spirits and their work showed  just how knowledgeable they were and how capable they were when working together. They were clean, no garbage just laying around. Garbage put right to the plastic garbage bag. Quite a team!

Every aspect of this experience, the initial call, the visit by Elite's sales rep. Victor (the owner) doing his best to get the work done when he said it would be done and Logan and Ozzie. Could not ask for anything more straight forward. This company obviously believes in customer service and that initiates loyalty from their customers. I, for one, am loyal customer to Elite. As I said at the beginning. A great experience.</Review>

Their "technician" was able to come out two days later, fiddled around the unit for about twenty minutes, then told my son that he didn't have the equipment to do any testing, and that he didn't know what to do anyway. He said that  blower motor parts would cost $1500, and that we had no warranty because we hadn't purchased their Maintenance Program. He left, after charging our son $65, and saying another tech would be by two days from then. I retrieved the unearned $65 later!
I checked with Yelp, and found that Elite Comfort Systems  was top-rated. I called and left a message. Soon, I received a call from Vic, the owner. He was able to come out that day, and complete all needed testing, and determined that the blower motor and related circuit boards needed replacement. It took two weeks for the factory (Day and Night) to deliver the parts to Vic, but as soon as they arrived, he sent his tech, Joe, to our home. In a short time, Joe had the A/C humming again.  I have many years experience as a mechanic, technician, and superintendent with P.G.&E. I would have welcomed a person of Joe's quality into my organization. He is well educated, and experienced despite his young years. He explained the repairs as he was doing them. A very smooth and organized worker with great work ethics. Alex did most of the servicing, he explained what he was doing and based on the age of the unit and what he observed, gave us his recommendations for servicing and repair. Of course our unit was on its best behavior when they got there but Alex explained how the furnace and AC Unit work in tandem and what may have potentially made the crazy sounds. He was very fourth coming with educating us and answering our questions.

Upon arrival both Alex and Robert wore masks and when Alex entered our house to check the furnace, which is located in the Attic he immediately wore booties on his shoes.

They came for a service call, did a unit check-up, educated us and answered our questions, we're first time home buyers, so there were a lot. We felt they weren't pushy salesmen that were trying to milk us for every dollar. They assessed our situation, let us know what our current situation was, suggested some repairs and maintenance to help prolong the life of our unit. Then left it up up to us to decide, no scare tactics or high pressure sales. Thank You Elite again for addressing our concerns. And we'll see you in the fall.<//Review>

< text>
Antime you get involve in a major project, you just never really know who to call. My HVAC system' which was installed in 2002' failed. It was over 103 degrees that day and would be that hot for next few days. I called the original installer of my system. They were quite capable and when this company checked the system, it was time for a new one. Elite got out the house the next day and came to same conclusion.

I called the original installer and they said they would send a rep to go over the cost and set up a time to install. Then the phone rep said that a install couldn't happen for a month. I told them that would not work and thanked them for their time. Enter Elite.

Chianti came to the house and was very low keyed. No pressure, just wanted to show what was needed. I felt comfortable but I had to ask. When can you install? Chianti call Victor, the owner. Victor said that they could install by the end of the week. I told Chianti that I had called another company to look the system over and to quote me a price. In fact, they showed up as Chianti was leaving.

I waited until the next day to compare prices. The second company was more expensive but pushed financing (which I did not need) and the ability to match prices. I thanked them for their time, call Chianti and signed the contract to have Elite install. Great decision on my part.

Three days later at 8:30 am, Logan and Ozzie were at the front door. Showed them to the system and they went to work. They even had a moment or two to play fetch with my dogs! First day, the entire system was removed. Second day, back at 8:30 for the install. That afternoon we had one outstanding HVAC system blowing cold air.

There two guys were great. I asked questions (I work from home), they answered them. They were always in good spirits and their work showed  just how knowledgeable they were and how capable they were when working together. They were clean, no garbage just laying around. Garbage put right to the plastic garbage bag. Quite a team!

Every aspect of this experience, the initial call, the visit by Elite's sales rep. Victor (the owner) doing his best to get the work done when he said it would be done and Logan and Ozzie. Could not ask for anything more straight forward. This company obviously believes in customer service and that initiates loyalty from their customers. I, for one, am loyal customer to Elite. As I said at the beginning. A great experience.<//text>

< text>
I have used Elite several times and have had an excellent experience each time. I have found them to be problem solvers—finding out what is truly wrong and fixing only what’s needed, not just adding extra things that aren’t needed to pad the bill. My latest experience was when my home warranty company sent out a company I wasn’t familiar with, but I had no choice, and they came back with several major repairs that were going to cost thousands. I sought out a second opinion with Elite on my own, and after testing the most obvious thing (the starter) so that the other problems could be diagnosed, it turned out the starter was dead. After replacing it on the spot, my A/C worked perfectly right away! Needless to say, the repair was just a few hundred dollars instead of thousands or a system replacement. I will never use anyone else. They truly are Elite!<//text>

< Review>
My furnace and air conditioner are only a year old, but I understand the importance of preventative maintenance. The Elite representative was right on time. He explained the annual maintenance contract and the alternative option of calling as needed. I went with the annual contract, based on our homebuilder’s recommendation.

The representative checked the furnace operation, changed the filter and cleaned up the accumulated dust. He also checked the thermostat to be sure it worked properly. Next, he inspected and cleaned the air conditioning unit, pointing out to me that the homebuilder had not secured it to its base. Finally, he checked to be sure the air conditioner was  working properly.

The representative was efficient, knowledgeable (with 7 years of experience) courteous and performed the work very well. I would definitely recommend Elite, and I will use them in the future.< /Review>
